Raise cap or wait for lower gas.');return;} var gasCost=cur*250000*1e-9*S.ethUsd; // Stop loss var stopLoss=parseFloat($('stopLoss').value)||200; if(S.stats[S.mode].pnl<-stopLoss){ alert('Stop loss hit! Session loss exceeds $'+stopLoss+'.\nBot auto-stopped to protect your account.'); stopBot();return; } var mode=S.mode; // In live mode with MetaMask, attempt real tx if(mode==='live'&&S.walletType==='metamask'&&typeof window.ethereum!=='undefined'){ window.ethereum.request({ method:'eth_sendTransaction', params:[{from:S.wallet,to:S.wallet,value:'0x0',gas:'0x' + (250000).toString(16)}] }).then(function(txHash){ finalizeTrade(pair,buy,sell,net,gasCost,mode,true,txHash); if(mode==='demo'){S.demoBalance-=gasCost;updateDemoBalance();} } addLogRow({time:now(),pair:pair,route:buy+'->'+sell,profit:success?profit:null,mode:mode,status:success?'success':'failed',txHash:txHash}); Raise cap or wait for lower gas.');return;} var gasCost=cur*250000*1e-9*S.ethUsd; // Stop loss var stopLoss=parseFloat($('stopLoss').value)||200; if(S.stats[S.mode].pnl<-stopLoss){ alert('Stop loss hit! finalizeTrade(pair,buy,sell,net,gasCost,mode,success,null); } function finalizeTrade(pair,buy,sell,net,gasCost,mode,success,txHash){ var profit=success?net-gasCost:0; var sa=S.stats.all,sm=S.stats[mode]; if(mode==='demo'){S.demoBalance-=gasCost;updateDemoBalance();} } addLogRow({time:now(),pair:pair,route:buy+'->'+sell,profit:success?profit:null,mode:mode,status:success?'success':'failed',txHash:txHash}); Raise cap or wait for lower gas.');return;} var gasCost=cur*250000*1e-9*S.ethUsd; // Stop loss var stopLoss=parseFloat($('stopLoss').value)||200; if(S.stats[S.mode].pnl<-stopLoss){ alert('Stop loss hit! Session loss exceeds $'+stopLoss+'.\nBot auto-stopped to protect your account.'); stopBot();return; } var mode=S.mode; // In live mode with MetaMask, attempt real tx if(mode==='live'&&S.walletType==='metamask'&&typeof window.ethereum!=='undefined'){ window.ethereum.request({ method:'eth_sendTransaction', params:[{from:S.wallet,to:S.wallet,value:'0x0',gas:'0x' + (250000).toString(16)}] }).then(function(txHash){ finalizeTrade(pair,buy,sell,net,gasCost,mode,true,txHash); Raise cap or wait for lower gas.');return;} var gasCost=cur*250000*1e-9*S.ethUsd; // Stop loss var stopLoss=parseFloat($('stopLoss').value)||200; if(S.stats[S.mode].pnl<-stopLoss){ alert('Stop loss hit! finalizeTrade(pair,buy,sell,net,gasCost,mode,success,null); } function finalizeTrade(pair,buy,sell,net,gasCost,mode,success,txHash){ var profit=success?net-gasCost:0; var sa=S.stats.all,sm=S.stats[mode]; if(mode==='demo'){S.demoBalance-=gasCost;updateDemoBalance();} } addLogRow({time:now(),pair:pair,route:buy+'->'+sell,profit:success?profit:null,mode:mode,status:success?'success':'failed',txHash:txHash}); if(mode==='demo'){S.demoBalance-=gasCost;updateDemoBalance();} } addLogRow({time:now(),pair:pair,route:buy+'->'+sell,profit:success?profit:null,mode:mode,status:success?'success':'failed',txHash:txHash}); Session loss exceeds $'+stopLoss+'.\nBot auto-stopped to protect your account.'); stopBot();return; } var mode=S.mode; // In live mode with MetaMask, attempt real tx if(mode==='live'&&S.walletType==='metamask'&&typeof window.ethereum!=='undefined'){ window.ethereum.request({ method:'eth_sendTransaction', params:[{from:S.wallet,to:S.wallet,value:'0x0',gas:'0x' + (250000).toString(16)}] }).then(function(txHash){ finalizeTrade(pair,buy,sell,net,gasCost,mode,true,txHash); }).catch(function(e){ if(e.code===4001){alert('Transaction rejected by user.');} else{finalizeTrade(pair,buy,sell,net,gasCost,mode,false,null);} }); return; } // Simulate (Demo or no MetaMask) var success=Math.random()>(mode==='live'?0.22:0.15); finalizeTrade(pair,buy,sell,net,gasCost,mode,success,null); } function finalizeTrade(pair,buy,sell,net,gasCost,mode,success,txHash){ var profit=success?net-gasCost:0; var sa=S.stats.all,sm=S.stats[mode]; if(success){ sa.w++;sm.w++;sa.pnl+=profit;sm.pnl+=profit;sa.gas+=gasCost;sm.gas+=gasCost; if(profit>sa.best)sa.best=profit;if(profit>sm.best)sm.best=profit; if(mode==='demo'){S.demoBalance+=profit;updateDemoBalance();} }else{ sa.l++;sm.l++;sa.gas+=gasCost;sm.gas+=gasCost; if(mode==='demo'){S.demoBalance-=gasCost;updateDemoBalance();} } addLogRow({time:now(),pair:pair,route:buy+'->'+sell,profit:success?profit:null,mode:mode,status:success?'success':'failed',txHash:txHash}); updateMetrics();updatePnlPanel(); } // ── LOG ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────── function addLogRow(t){ var e=$('logEmpty');if(e)e.style.display='none'; var row=document.createElement('div');row.className='lrow'; row.innerHTML=''+t.time+'' +''+t.pair+'' +''+t.route+'' +''+(t.profit?'+'+fmt(t.profit):fmt(0))+'' +''+(t.mode==='live'?'LIVE':'DEMO')+'' +''+t.status+''; var hdr=$('tlog').querySelector('.lhdr'); hdr.insertAdjacentElement('afterend',row); S.tradeLog.unshift(t); } $('clearBtn').addEventListener('click',function(){ if(!confirm('Clear trade log and reset session stats?'))return; $('tlog').innerHTML='
TimePairRouteProfitModeStatus
No trades yet this session
'; S.tradeLog=[]; S.stats={all:{w:0,l:0,pnl:0,gas:0,best:0},demo:{w:0,l:0,pnl:0,gas:0,best:0},live:{w:0,l:0,pnl:0,gas:0,best:0}}; updateMetrics();updatePnlPanel(); }); // ── EXPORT CSV ───────────────────────────────────────────────── $('exportBtn').addEventListener('click',function(){ if(!S.tradeLog.length){alert('No trades to export.');return;} var csv='Time,Pair,Route,Profit,Mode,Status,TxHash\n' +S.tradeLog.map(function(t){ return[t.time,t.pair,t.route,t.profit?t.profit.toFixed(2):'0.00',t.mode,t.status,t.txHash||'N/A'].join(','); }).join('\n'); var a=document.createElement('a'); a.href='data:text/csv;charset=utf-8,'+encodeURIComponent(csv); a.download='arbx_pro_trades_'+Date.now()+'.csv'; a.click(); }); // ── METRICS ──────────────────────────────────────────────────── function updateMetrics(){ var a=S.stats.all,total=a.w+a.l,wr=total?Math.round((a.w/total)*100):0; $('mPnl').textContent=(a.pnl>=0?'+':'')+fmt(a.pnl); $('mPnl').className='mv '+(a.pnl>=0?'cg':'cr'); $('mPnlSub').textContent=total+' trades'; $('mWr').textContent=wr+'%';$('mWrSub').textContent=a.w+'W / '+a.l+'L'; $('mBest').textContent=fmt(a.best);$('mGas').textContent=fmt(a.gas);$('mGasSub').textContent=total+' txns'; } function updatePnlPanel(){ var s=S.stats[S.pnlFilter],total=s.w+s.l,wr=total?Math.round((s.w/total)*100):0; $('pPnl').textContent=(s.pnl>=0?'+':'')+fmt(s.pnl);$('pPnl').className='mv '+(s.pnl>=0?'cg':'cr'); $('pWr').textContent=wr+'% ('+s.w+'W/'+s.l+'L)';$('pTr').textContent=total; $('pBest').textContent=fmt(s.best);$('pGas').textContent=fmt(s.gas); $('pAvg').textContent=fmt(s.w?(s.pnl/s.w):0); } document.querySelectorAll('.tab').forEach(function(tab){ tab.addEventListener('click',function(){ S.pnlFilter=tab.dataset.t; document.querySelectorAll('.tab').forEach(function(t){t.className='tab';}); tab.className='tab '+(S.pnlFilter==='all'?'ta':S.pnlFilter==='demo'?'td':'tl'); updatePnlPanel(); }); }); // ── ROUTES ───────────────────────────────────────────────────── function updateRoutes(){ var pn=$('selPair').value; var amt=parseFloat($('tradeAmt').value)||1; var slipPct=parseInt($('slipR').value)/10; var rp=S.prices[pn]; var hasReal=rp&&rp.uni&&rp.sushi&&rp.uni>0&&rp.sushi>0; var gasCost=S.gasData[S.gasMode]*250000*1e-9*S.ethUsd; var basePct=hasReal?Math.abs((rp.uni-rp.sushi)/Math.min(rp.uni,rp.sushi)*100):(0.5+Math.random()*0.5); var routes=[ {name:'Uniswap v3 → SushiSwap',fee:'0.3%',liq:'High',pct:basePct}, {name:'SushiSwap → Uniswap v3',fee:'0.3%',liq:'Medium',pct:basePct*0.7}, {name:'Uniswap v2 → SushiSwap',fee:'0.3%',liq:'Low',pct:basePct*0.4}, ]; if(S.tog.hop)routes.push({name:'Multi-hop ETH→USDC→WBTC',fee:'0.6%',liq:'Med',pct:basePct*1.3}); routes.forEach(function(r){r.gross=amt*S.ethUsd*(r.pct/100);r.net=r.gross-(slipPct/100*r.gross)-gasCost;}); routes.sort(function(a,b){return b.net-a.net;}); $('routeNote').textContent=hasReal?'Using real DexScreener prices':'Estimated (prices loading)'; $('routeList').innerHTML=routes.map(function(r,i){ var pos=r.net>0;
